Oxanium ExtraLight Regular (Oxanium-ExtraLight.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Oxanium' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraLight' = NID 1 'Oxanium ExtraLight'.

Mac name table entries are not necessary anymore.

This font has no Mac name table entries. This is correct.
Further read: App test: no Mac name table

Pass

Oxanium Light Regular (Oxanium-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Oxanium-Light', Everything looks good.

Pass

Oxanium Light Regular (Oxanium-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
'space' in NID 6 cause issues in fontbook for Mac.

NID 6 is 'Oxanium-Light', Everything looks good.

Pass

Oxanium Light Regular (Oxanium-Light.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Oxanium' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Light' = NID 1 'Oxanium Light'.

Pass

Oxanium Medium Regular (Oxanium-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Oxanium-Medium', Everything looks good.

Pass

Oxanium Medium Regular (Oxanium-Medium.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Oxanium' + 'Space' + NID 17 'Medium' = NID 1 'Oxanium Medium'.

Pass

Oxanium SemiBold Regular (Oxanium-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Oxanium-SemiBold', Everything looks good.

Oxanium SemiBold Regular (Oxanium-SemiBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Oxanium' + 'Space' + NID 17 'SemiBold' = NID 1 'Oxanium SemiBold'.

Pass

Oxanium ExtraBold Regular (Oxanium-ExtraBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 6

MS NID 6, PostScript Name check for illegal characters.
Monotype uses NID 6 for creating CSS classes for their demo HTML. The following characters cause issues in the CSS code: '
, , , &, _, [, ], (, ), {, }, <, >, /, \, %'

NID 6 is 'Oxanium-ExtraBold', Everything looks good.

Oxanium ExtraBold Regular (Oxanium-ExtraBold.ttf)

name

MS NID 16/17

MS NID 16 + NID 17 should match NID 1 (+2).
Otherwise cross platform compatibility does not work between Mac (uses NID 16+17) and Windows (uses NID 1+2). (Jan 2019)

NID 16 'Oxanium' + 'Space' + NID 17 'ExtraBold' = NID 1 'Oxanium ExtraBold'.
